# All In-Game Help Pages

Complete dump of all 1505 help pages from `script.gcg`.

Pages are in the order they appear in the Lua scripts.

---

## 1. Mini Map, Zodiac World Map, Map, Route

Map
Click [M] at top left corner of the interface or press  shortcut [Tab]to open map.

Map Function
 Every Round Mark at the map locates a NPC. They are marked with different colors according to their careers. By clicking [Quest] and [Function], the map will show Quest Npc and Function Npc. By clicking [NPC List], you can check NPC name at the map.

Locate NPC
Move the mouse to one round mark at the map to check NPC name and coordinates. Click the round mark to locate the NPC.

World Map
Click [W] at top left corner of the Map or press  shortcut [Alt+M]to open Zodiac World Map.

---

## 2. Quest, Current Quests, Finished Quests, Idiom Collection, Abortion

Press  Shortcut [Alt+Q] to open Quest Panel. There are 3 sub-panels:[Quest Complete],[Current Quest] and [Card Collection]

Quest Complete
To check quest completion evaluation. S level is the top level.

Current Quest
Click quest name to check quest description.

Card Collection
When you go up to Level 20, you can go to speak with Cloud City--Corey to accept card collection quest. Card Collection Quest has 5 quests per day.  One quest  for one card.  Cards are attached with special effect which can be used in combat.

Quest Track
Open Quest Panel, click the incomplete quest  to show quest descriptions on the right.

Abandon Quest
On [Current Quest], select the quest you want to abandon and then click [Abandon Quest] on the panel.
 When you abandon the quest, you may need to do it from the start. Think before you leap!!

 Quest Panel Abbreviation Tips [M]--[Main Quest];[B]--[Branch Quest];[Z]--[Zodiac Quest];[E]--[Event Quest];[H]--[Holiday Quest];[G]--[Guild Quest];[R]--[Recycle Quest];[L]--[Marriage Quest];[C]--[Card Quest];[D]--[Daily Quest].

---

## 3. Character, Character Status, Adding Points, Fame , Character Fame

Shortcut key to open charactor panel:[ALT+C]

Status Point
+ 4 status points per level which can be added to Vitality, Intelligence, Strength and Dexterity.

Fame
Click [Fame] on Charactor Panel to check its Moral, Renown and Guilty.
    Go to speak with Cloud City--Thad to accept Renown Quest. After completing the former 20 steps of Renown Quest, you will be rewarded with double experience and Renown points. If a player logs off immediately after completing a Renown quest, he/she shall wait until his/her renown is recovered before do the next renown quest when he/she logs in the game again. Or his previous renown value will be removed and covered.
Moral and Guilty is coming soon!

---

## 4. Pet, Pet's Food, Pet's Attributes, Pet Talent, Pet Freedom, Pet Health

Shortcut to open Pet Panel: [ALT+W]

Summon Pet
Click [Summon] on Pet Panel,your pet will enter into the combat. If pet's level is higher than its owner, it will not join in the combat.

Pet Status Point
  + 4 Status points per level which can be added to Vitality, Intelligence, Strength and Dexterity.

Release Pet
Click [Release ] on Pet Panel to release your current pet.

Pet Health
Initial Health of Pet is 1000. Health will reduce when it combats, flees,or be killed. You can go to locate Cloud City--Pet Curer for Pet Health Potion.

Pet Talent
Click [Pet Talent] on Pet Panel to check pet talent status,pet item and pet skill.  F7-F8 are pet's fixed shortcuts.

Pet Show
Click [Set Pet Info] on pet panel and then press enter to show your pet in chat box.

---

## 5. Team, Team Panel, New Team, Promotion, Dismission, Step Out, Team Invite, Return to Team, Team Infor.

Create Team
Click [Create Team] on team panel to create your team.

Invite To Team
There are at most 5 members in a team. Team leader can receive invitations from other players when there are not 5 members. Team leader can accept new members from [Applicants] on the left of Team Panel. Click  Accept  to accept players application and add them into teammates list. Click [Refuse] to refuse an applicatioin. Team Leader can invite other players by right-click the player. Click \"Invite To Team\".
When there are 5 members, team will not receive other players application.

Promote to Leader
  Team Leader can promote any member to be team leader.

Remove Member
Team leader can remove team members when not in combat scene.

Quit Team
Team leader will guide team member to walk. Team members can click [Quit] to quit team.
When quitting, a player can not be back.

Team Info
You can open this panel. Function will be available soon.

---

## 6. Pack, Equipment Panel, Heal&Medicine, Change Equipment

Shortcut to open Pack Panel:[ALT+E]

Item Bar
Click \"Bag\" to show your bag and charactor's item bar. Click Hide to close and open item bar. Click Hide again to open charactor's clothes bar. Click Clothes to switch to item panel. Click  Pet  icon at top left corner of charactor item panel to switch to pet item panel.

Change Item
Be sure it is charactor's item panel rather than clothes panel or pet panel when you want to replace items. Right click weapon and armor in  Item Sack to change items in Item Panel.
    Press  Pet  icon to switch to pet item panel and right click pet item to change it. TipPet item can not be removed after equipment. New item will replace the previous item and the previous will disappear.
    When people need to equip new clothes, click  Clothes icon to switch to clothes panel and right click it to equip.

Heal Charactor
Right click potions in Sack to heal charactor or pet on the left.

Sort Item
 Click[Sort] button in the item sack to automatically sort items inside.

---

## 7. Skill, Skill System, Skills Level, Skills Study, Skills Upgrading, Shortcuts of Skills

Press  Shortcut [ALT+S] to open skill panel.

Skill Type
There are Aptitude Skill, Normal Skill, Zodiac Skill, Passive Skill and Additional Skill.

Skill Train
Aptitude Skill: Aptitude Skill are skills of the aptitude you chose while creating your charactor. Click [Aptitude] to view all aptitude skills on the panel.Aptitude Skill can be upgraded to 12 level. LocateGrocerandFreddie to buy Gr.1 and Gr.2 skill books. You can accept Monster Encyclopedia quest to loote Gr.3 and Gr.4 Skill books at your 30 level.
    Normal Skill: All non-aptitude skills are normal skills. Normal skills can be learned from skill books. Normal skill can be upgraded to level 10.LocateGrocerandFreddie to buy Gr.1 and Gr.2 skill books. You can accept Monster Encyclopedia quest to loot Gr.3 and Gr.4 Skill books at your 30 level.
    Passive Skill:  Passive skill are closely related with Aptitude skill and normal skill. Passive skill will grow automatically with upgrading of aptitude and normal skill. Aptitude passive skill can be upgraded 1 level higher than normal passive skill.
    Zodiac Skill:At your 25 level, you can locate Cloud City--Commander to acceptZodiac MissionQuest. When you complete a quest,you will be rewarded a Zodiac skill. Zodiac skill consists of 2 types: attack skill(Metal, Water, Fire and Wood) and control skill.
    Additional Skill: Gathering skill, living skill, marriage skill and brothership skill are additional skills. These skills can not be learned from skill books. You can learn gathering skill and living skill from Housewife( refer to gathering system and living system for details.) Marriage skill and brotherhood skill will be mastered when the needed relationship are established.

Skill Grade
 Aptitude skill and normal skill are closely related with status. They shall obey the following roles.
    There are 6 grades for each skill and 3 skills for each grade. You can only learn 1 skill from the 3.[Gray Skill Icon] You can not learn it now.[Colorful Skill Icon]You have mastered it.

Skill Shortcut
Mastered skill be been shown in Mastered Skill Panel. Drag its icon into shortcut bar(F2-F6) on game interface to setup shortcuts.

---

## 8. Skill, Skill System, Skills Level, Skills Study, Skills Upgrading, Shortcuts of Skills

Press  Shortcut [ALT+S] to open skill panel.

Skill Type
There are Aptitude Skill, Normal Skill, Zodiac Skill, Passive Skill and Additional Skill.

Skill Train
Aptitude Skill: Aptitude Skill are skills of the aptitude you chose while creating your charactor. Click [Aptitude] to view all aptitude skills on the panel.Aptitude Skill can be upgraded to 12 level. LocateGrocerandFreddie to buy Gr.1 and Gr.2 skill books. You can accept Monster Encyclopedia quest to loote Gr.3 and Gr.4 Skill books at your 30 level.
    Normal Skill: All non-aptitude skills are normal skills. Normal skills can be learned from skill books. Normal skill can be upgraded to level 10.LocateGrocerandFreddie to buy Gr.1 and Gr.2 skill books. You can accept Monster Encyclopedia quest to loote Gr.3 and Gr.4 Skill books at your 30 level.
    Passive Skill:  Passive skill are closely related with Aptitude skill and normal skill. Passive skill will grow automatically with upgrading of aptitude and normal skill. Aptitude passive skill can be upgraded 1 level higher than normal passive skill.
    Zodiac Skill:At your 25 level, you can locate Cloud City--Commander to acceptZodiac MissionQuest. When you complete a quest,you will be rewarded a Zodiac skill. Zodiac skill consists of 2 types: attack skill(Metal, Water, Fire and Wood) and control skill.
    Additional Skill: Gathering skill, living skill, marriage skill and brothership skill are additional skills. These skills can not be learned from skill books. You can learn gathering skill and living skill from Housewife( refer to gathering system and living system for details.) Marriage skill and brotherhood skill will be mastered when the needed relationship are established.

Skill Grade
 Aptitude skill and normal skill are closely related with status. They shall obey the following roles.
    There are 6 grades for each skill and 3 skills for each grade. You can only learn 1 skill from the 3.[Gray Skill Icon] You can not learn it now.[Colorful Skill Icon]You have mastered it.

Skill Shortcut
Mastered skill be been shown in Mastered Skill Panel. Drag its icon into shortcut bar(F2-F6) on game interface to setup shortcuts.

---

## 9. Relation, Add Friends, Chat, Friends Order, Mentor

Shortcut to open Relationship Panel: [ALT+F]

Add Friend
Click  Magnifiericon on Relationship Panel.Enter in player name and fill in message.Then click  Send . With the other's permit, he/she will be added in your friend list.

Friend Chat
Click Friendicon on Relation Panel to show Friend List. Click Friend() to show a drop down friend list. Double click the friend you want to chat with, a chat box will pop up.

Friend Option
Friend Option consists:Detailed Info, Remove, Drag to Blacklist, Remove from Blacklist and Mentor. Right click friend icon. Choose the option in drop down box.

Mentor
Right click friend icon and choose Mentor . When your request is accepted, your relationship became mentor and student. Meanwhile your information will be removed to Mentor and student list.

---

## 10. Relation, Add Friends, Chat, Friends Order, Mentor

Shortcut to open Relationship Panel: [ALT+F]

Add Friend
Click  Magnifiericon on Relationship Panel.Enter in player name and fill in message.Then click  Send . With the other's permit, he/she will be added in your friend list.

Friend Chat
Click Friendicon on Relation Panel to show Friend List. Click Friend() to show a drop down friend list. Double click the friend you want to chat with, a chat box will pop up.

Friend Option
Friend Option consists:Detal Info, Remove, Drag to Blacklist, Remove from Blacklist and Mentor. Right click friend icon. Choose the option in drop down box.

Mentor
Right click friend icon and choose Mentor . When your request is accepted, your relationship became mentor and student. Meanwhile your information will be removed to Mentor and student list.

---

## 11. Fight, Attack, Skill, Item, Defense, Escape, Summon, Auto

Skill
 Click Skill button to show all mastered skills. Select a skill and left click it to attack your foe. Capture Pet button under  Skill  icon is the skill to capture a zodiac animal in combat to be your pet.

Item
Click  Item  button to open Item Sack interface. In combat, you can heal your charactor or pet through this function.

Defense
Click Defense button in combat to protect your charactor or pet.

Flee
Click Flee button in combat to sneak away. You will quit the team while fleeing under team status. There is chance of fleeing failed.

Summon
Click Summon button in combat to call your pet. One pet can only be summoned once per combat. Low health point of pet may lead to a failed summon.

Auto
Click  Auto button in combat to repeat last attack method. In a combat,[TAB] is shortcut of Auto.


Last Page

---

## 12. Chat, Chat Channel, Chat Tool,

Chat Channel
Click World channel on Chat Box to show other chat channels. Tick all chat channels and the Chat Wizard Box will show all chatting info. Tick off one chat channel, the Chat Wizard will shield this channel info.

Chat Wizard
 Click [Change Background] Button at top of Chat Wizard to change background color.

Chat Expression
Click [Insert Expression] button on Chat Bar to insert expression from expression panel.

Private Chat
Click [Private Chat] button on Chat Bar to show private chat history.

Text Color
> Click [Change Color] button on Chat Bar to change text color.


Last Page

---

## 13. Brotherhood, Brotherhood Quests, Requirement for Brotherhood, Rules for Brotherhood

Brotherhood Requirement
The 2 players shall make a team(2 member only) and locate Brotherhood Manager to accept brotherhood task.

Brotherhood Rule
If one party of the 2 abandon the quest, quit the team or log off, the quest fails.

Brotherhood Quest
  Thick and Thin
Make a team and kill Enchanted Vampire.Then back to NPC to submit quest.
  Blood Oath
Kill Elite Goblin to bring Chain of Brotherhood back to NPC.
Your brotherhood is tested and you are brothers now!!

---

## 14. Marriage, Requirements for Marriage, Rules for Marriage, Quest for Marriage

Marriage Requirement
The 2 payers shall make a team(2 members only) and locate Match-Maker  to accept marriage quest.

Marriage Rule
If one party of the 2 abandon the quest, quit the team or log off, the quest fails.

Marriage Quest
Common Enemy
Make a team and kill Jade Beast. Get Exquisite Stone back. Submit quest to NPC.
Common Challenge
Kill Ghost Fiend and back to NPC. NPC will give you a Keepsake.
Wedding Dress
 Bring the keepsake to Fairy lynn.Fairy Lynn needs Snow Sachet to weave the wedding dress with magic power of love.
Bride Veil
Joint efforts to kill Enchanted Beast and bring Snow Sachet to Fairy Lynn. Fairy Lynn will give you a Rainbow Garment in return.
Joint Hands
 Bring the Rainbow Garment to Match-Maker. Match-Maker will witness your true love and hold your wedding party!!

---

## 15. Page 15

Mob FlaskClick [Item] button in combat and right click [Mob Flask]. Then left click the monster you want to capture to seal the evil. Move the mouse to the vase to show monster info.
    Mob Flaskis divided according to various levels. Different level genie vase can be used to capture monsters of different levels!!

## 16. Page 16

Fate System
A hidden attribute attached with Zodiac Envoy. Whether he is male or female, so long as the doomed fate is seen,it is doomed, precious! When you met your lover, do not let him/her go. Be good friends and get closer in future!
    Help Elf: refer to [Help] for Friend Panel operation!

---

## 17. God

Fairy becomes incarnate!!Jade Emperor send God of Bless, God of Misfortune,God of Wealth and God of Poorness to earth for patrol!! Gods may make troubles or tests to hero to reduce their experience or money.Come on and tand the test, Heros!!

Attention~Attention~! You are confer with this title for your excellent performance on Zodiac journey!
 Help Elf: Open Charactor Panel and dounle click box biside the title to choose a content.

## 19. Trade

Click [ Sell ] and then click item in Item Sack to sell it to store.

Click [Buy] and then click item in store to buy it.

Click [Repair] and then click item in item panel or item sack to repair them.

Click [Repair All] to repair all items in item panel. N/A for items in item sack!

---

## 20. Perfect Attack

Perfect Kill~!!Excellent Job~Check your reward~!!

## 21. Page 21

If your quest is failed, do not give up! Open [Quest Panel--Shortcut ALT+Q] to choose the failed quest and then click[Abandon Quest] to locate designated NPC to accept it again!!

Thus all creatures on earth are getting ready for a fight to became the chosen.Apollo descends to the world to find candidates. The road ahead is tortuous. You have to make great efforts to became one of the envoys. Please take the Zodiac Recommendation to find Blacksmith. Blacksmith is now at the entrance to the village.

## 45. Passing the Love, Maria, Hubbert, Sachet, Lvl.8

"[Quest #354]"

Quest Level: 8
Start NPC: "[NPC #3028]"  "[Map #103]".
End NPC: "[NPC #3030]"  "[Map #112]".

## 428. Collection

Gather System

Mentor NPCCloud CityHousewife

    Guidence: learning it consumes Renown points to learn gather skills. The 1st gathering skill is for free. The 2nd gather skill will consume 300 Renown Points. The 3rd gathering skill will consume 600 Renown Points.

    Type: Mine, Lumber, Medicine, Fish(Coming Soon) and ect.

    Method: Buy corresponding gathering tool from Housewife and put on it after finding materials. Double click the material to gather.
Tip: Gather will stop when gather tool's durability reduces to 0 or the pack is full.

---

## 429. War of Divine Animal

War of Divine Animal System

Mentor NPC: Cloud City--War of Divine Animal Teleporter

    Event Requirement:
    Player shall be above 20 level (20 included).
    There shall be more than 3 members in the team.

    Event time: Monday--Friday 000 C 21:30
    Player can enter into the game once per day. On Friday, Player need a Starry Key to enter.

    Content:  There are 14 passes for you to challenge within Monday to Thursday. Kill the 14 guards to complete the quest. Degree of difficulty:
    There are 4 Divine Animals on Friday. Kill them to complete your quest. Degree of difficulty:

    Event Reward: Accept rewards from War of Divine Animal Gate Keeper.
    Monday:   Vermilion Bird Xanadu    Item Reward: Private Key of Vermilion Bird Xanadu
    Tuesday   Black Tortoise Xanadu    Item Reward: Private Key of Black Tortoise Xanadu
    Wednesday   Blue Dragon Xanadu    Item Reward: Private Key of Blue Dragon Xanadu
    Thursday   White Tiger Xanadu    Item Reward: Private Key of White Tiger Xanadu
    Accept your reward at War of Divine Animal Gate Keeper's. The player who did not complete whoe quest can accept corresponding pass reward.(One boss per pass)
    On Friday, you can accept double experience reward from Gate Keeper.

## 431. Guild Quest

Guild Quest
    Daily Quest: Guild owner or vice guild owner can release daily quest per day. The quest will be randomly sent to online guild member. The acceptance member shall return to guild to complete guild quest at Presbyter Blair's. Members can also abandon the quest at quest panel. The quest will be randomly sent to another member.
Reward:

    Weekly Quest: Guild owner or vice guild owner can release weekly quest once per week. Weekly quest will be updated at Wendesday per week. It consists of several sub quests. Guild Owner or vice owner can release quest according to guild development.
Reward: Individual experience after quest and mana stone after weekly quest.

    Normal Quest: Accept normal quest at guild--Manager Emerson's. There are basic, senior and advanced normal quests.  Guild member can accept at most 5 times normal quest. Higher guild title can get accept more normal guild quest. The up-limit of normal quest is 21.
Reward: Individual experience and guild contribution after quest. You will get guild contribution , guild gold and individual experience after 3 quests. There is also a chance to get guild material and item reward. Reward item will be kept in guild warehouse. Guild member can exchange it by contribution. You can not see reward item status in warehouse. You can check it after getting it.

ChatAdviceClick to check

  Go to human world at ApolloChat Face
Click Face Insert, you can choose whatever faces you like.

Chat Channel
    Click World Channel which can show up many different other chat channels. You cant see the chat information until you check before the Chat Channel.

Chat Sprite
Click Change Background, you can change the color of the Chat Column
#Personal Chat
Click Personal List, you can see the players youve chatted with lately.

Word Color
Click  Change Color, you can change words color.

All about mapAdviceClick to check

  Go to human world at Apollo.The Map
There is a green M icon in the upper left corner of the window. Click on it and you will see the mini-map. You can also press Tab

Map Function
The round dot indicates the location of an NPC. Click on Quest above the map, and you can see where to accept quests. Click on Function to view the location of the quest NPCs. Click on Delivery to learn where the Delivery Spots are.

Search for NPC
Open the mini-map, move your cursor over a round dot, and you can see the coordinates of that NPC. Left click on the dot, and your character will move to that NPC automatically.

World Map
Click on World in the Mini-map panel to have a brief look at the world of Zodiac Online.

<Quest>How to pick ZodiacYou've already got that!!

Oops, I forgot to give this to Alphonso. No wander I didn't see him on Guild Convention!!

Learn Skill
You can buy Skill Book Bag from Grocer. She likes to study those odd things. You also have to meet certain requirements.

Skill Phrase
    Every skill can be classified into 6 phrases. Each phrase has 3 skills. You can choose only one skill to learn in each phrase.[Gray Mark] means you don't have the ability to learn this skill yet. [Colored Mark] means you've learnt that skill.

Upgrade Skill
Initiative Skill will upgrade according to the numbers you use it. Passive Skill will upgrade according to your Initiative Skill.

Shortcut Key
Use mouse to move Learnt Skill to Shortcut column, you can tap shortcut key to use skill.

Fight InstructionDetails: Click to check

  Go to Human World at Apollo.Skill
Click Skill, you can see all the skills youve learnt. Choose one skill and left-click to attack the monster. Click Catch Animal when fighting, you can catch the animal. Then it can be the Player's pet.

Item
Click Item , you can see the interface of items and you can treat your pet and yourself when fighting.

Defense
Click Defense, you can protect yourself and pet.

Escape
Click Escape, you can run away from the battle field. When in a team, if you choose escape, the team will break up.

Call
Click Call, you can get your pet fight with you. Each pet can be called once a time. Pet's Health Point will affect its fighting ability.

Auto
Click Auto, you can repeat the action you've done before. In the battle, [TAB] is the shortcut key to use Auto.

Reason of War


says: I support.This is all my fault. One year ago, I went hunting on the hill and wanted to catch a fox for my mother. Unfortunately I got stuck due to bad weather and dropped into a cave. When I woke up, I found a fox right sitting beside me. After then I know that it was his owner who saved me. Her name is Nalan. During the days in cave, she cooked for me and we talked a lot until my maids found me.

Do you fall for that girl?I can feel it when I saw her. When I came back I told everything to my father. He decided to take me to propose. Father said that Nalan must be a blue blood, so I must also try to act like a blue blood.


Why did the war break out?The king in Nalan State was very hospitable when we got there. However, that was just a trick. They imprisoned my father and threatened that if I didnt bring the Rainbow Stone to them, they would never release my father and never let me marry Nalan.


What's Rainbow Stone?It would be much easier if I knew what Rainbow Stone is. It is said that the stone has a very magic power. Anyone sees it and then makes a wish, his or her dream will come true. And the history also tells us that the Rainbow Stone belongs to the people in Celestial State. But it is only a legend, no one really knows where it is.


Did God of Venus help you?Several months later, I failed to bring the Stone. They breached the agreement and waged a war on us. We were not that strong, but still, we could reduce the damage at the minimu. They were unhappy about the result and sent powerful witches to strengthen their forces. We were completely defeated. A few days before, my mother had a dream that Jade Emperor would send God of Venus to help us. Actually the dream came true.


Do you still love Nalan? I thought a lot and I believe She must have not a finger in this incident. The strange thing is that I never saw Nalan when we were in Nalan State. There must be some secrets. Can you help me find out?

Parents are your backup at home and friends are your support when you are going around! Come to me if you wanna a high renown!
Instruction on Renown Quest:
1: No limit on quest-taking every day, Double Experience for first 20 quests. Rewards will slope down after you finish first 20 quests.
2: When you finish 20 quests in a row there is a reward of renown points. The system will increase your renown points according to your online time.
3: You can exchange renown points for gold, Treasure Map and skill proficiency.
4: If you finish fixed amount of daily quests for 5 days per week, you will get an extra reward.
5: Renown Quest are independent of Double Experience.
 Note: No more than 90 quests per day! If you abort the quest, the number of finished quests will be recalculated!

Guild members co-ordinated their efforts and finished their task!Welcome to Guild Quests

Guild Quests include daily quests, weekly quests and activity quests!

Daily QuestMembers at or above rank of Guild leader and Vice leader release quests at Presbyter Blair in Guild Chamber. The quests will be allocated to Guild members on line randomly. Members who receive the allocations should take the quests at Presbyter Blair immediately. System will pass on the quests to the other members on line in random order and so on and so on until all the quests are finished! (Guild Member who receives the quest aborts the it automatically if he/she doesnt take the quest in time! The quests will pass on to the other members automatically!) Guild will receive relevant sources reward after 10 quests are finished!

Weekly QuestsThere are weekly accumulating quests in Guild. They can be received at Presbyter Blair in Guild Chamber. If the daily accumulating quests meet the number of weekly quests, it will be regarded as weekly quest completed! Every Guild member will earn certain experience and contributions when he/she first completes the weekly quests! Guild will earn certain material rewards when accumulating quests are completed!

Activity QuestsStart the activity quests during the activity! It required to be completed by all the members in Guild!

Welcome to Guild Quests

Daily Quests
Members at or above rank of Guild leader and Vice leader release quests at Presbyter Blair in Guild Chamber. The quests will be allocated to Guild members on line randomly. Members who receive the allocations should take the quests at Presbyter Blair immediately. System will pass on the quests to the other members on line in random order and so on and so on until all the quests are finished! (Guild Member who receives the quest aborts the it automatically if he/she doesnt take the quest in time! The quests will pass on to the other members automatically!)

Instructions on Anti-devil Activity:
1: Start Time: Every Saturday afternoon from 13:00 to 16:00.
2: Level Required: Guild members at or above Lvl 20 can enter event scene at Presbyter Blair.
3: There are 4 Bosses in activity. The more Bosses you beat the more rewards you will get. But you can only take the rewards for one time. Its better to take rewards after youve beaten more Bosses.
4: The level of monsters you fighting with are at the average level of your Guild members. High level players can lead new players fight monsters together. That will be a easy fight.

You will earn additional Guild Contributions when you do something for Guild if you master Contribute Bonus Skill. Contribute Bonus  Skill Lvl 1 will offer you 5% additional contribution. 5% per level-up.

Learn Contribute Bonus Skill Lvl 1 needs 20000 gold.

Pay 20000 gold
Learn Contribute Bonus Skill Lvl 2 needs 40000 gold and 1 Guild gold.

Pay 40000 gold and 1 Guild gold
Learn Contribute Bonus Skill Lvl 3 needs 80000 gold and 1 Guild gold.

Pay 80000 gold and 1 Guild gold
Learn Contribute Bonus Skill Lvl 4 needs 120000 gold and 2 Guild gold.

Pay 120000 gold and 2 Guild gold
Learn Contribute Bonus Skill Lvl 5 needs 160000 gold and 2 Guild gold.

Pay 160000 gold and 2 Guild gold
Learn Contribute Bonus Skill Lvl 6 needs 200000 gold and 3 Guild gold.

Pay 200000 gold and 3 Guild gold
Learn Contribute Bonus Skill Lvl 7 needs 250000 gold and 4 Guild gold.

Pay 250000 gold and 4 Guild gold
Learn Contribute Bonus Skill Lvl 8 needs 300000 gold and 6 Guild gold.

Pay 300000 gold and 6 Guild gold
Learn Contribute Bonus Skill Lvl 9 needs 400000 gold and 8 Guild gold.

Pay 400000 gold and 8 Guild gold
Learn Contribute Bonus Skill Lvl 10 needs 80000 gold and 10 Guild gold.

Pay 800000 gold and 10 Guild gold
You have reached the highest level of Contribute Bonus Skill and no more courses for you!

You will earn additional Guild Contributions when you do something for Guild if you master Contribute Bonus Skill. Contribute Bonus  Skill Lvl 1 will offer you 5% additional contribution. 5% per level-up.

Please come next time when you get enough gold!Planting Instruction:
1: You can ask Guild Gardener to plan Immortal Tree when the garden is established. Once tree for one time.
2: Guild leader, Vice leader or Immortal Producer can sow Click sowing links and put the seeds into sowing box. When the sowing is completed there will be a tip for it.
3: Immortal Trees has its own life, level and harvest cycle. Immortal Tree will automatically upgrade by 1 level and Guild Warehouse will sow after a harvest!
4: In view of diverse trees, Immortal Tree will lose a bit of its life for one period. Use Fertilizers to prolong its life. When Immortal Trees life point down to 0, it gonna die and disappear automatically. Then you can sow a new tree.
5: When the highest level Immortal Tree yields fruit the tree will disappear automatically. Then you can sow a new tree.

     Fertilizing Instruction::
1: Guild members can spend gold at Guild Gardener on some fertilizers.
2: Right click fertilizers and move your mouse onto Immortal Tree. The curser will turn into watering mode. Under watering mode, left click to fertilize Immortal Trees.
3: Fertilizer will be ineffective when Immortal Tree is at highest level.You can find all the Immortal Trees for Guild planting here.

The activity explanation:
1:Demon Hole is open during 1 to 4 o'clock every Saturday afternoon and you will be teleported back if beyond that time.
2:There are four Bosses in Demon Hole: Venom TreeGhostly PigFantom Pig and Soul-Biting Corpse.
3:The reward you get depends on the number of Bosses you defeat and can be gotten only once. (Take note: Fantom Spider and Enchanted Tree are not Bosses.)
4: If you defeat Fantom Spider and Enchanted Tree who can be killed only once, you will get more experience and has a small chance to get Guild resources.
5:Be more careful about a monster with the level of above 80, which will be empowered greatly.

Do it laterNot enough space in your package. Please release some space first!You haven't got enough money. Please come here again when you do!Guild Task Introduction:
1: The number of Guild Tasks that can be had depends on the level of a Guild. The higher it is, the more tasks the Guild has.
2: Every time a guild task is completed, you'll contribute to the Guild, get a little EXP and be rewarded a Guild Gold plus additional Guild resources every 3 tasks.
3: Guild Tasks are divided into basic. medium (above 20 level of the Guild) and advanced (above 40 level of the Guild) ones.
4:Basic Guild Tasks are suitable for players at 10-30 level, medium ones for 30-60 level and advanced ones for more than 60 level.
5: When a task is accepted, the number of task acceptance increase 1. If the task fails or is given up, the number will not go back. Please consider difficulty of tasks before accepting them!

## 1499. -Diana to open compound panel. Place one clothes in £ÛPart£Ýand the other clothes in another [Part]. Then click [Compound]. New clothes will be put into your sack. #0<5>Tip:#0<0> The bag shall have enough space. 2 10-level clothes can be compounded to a 30 level clothes. 2 30-level and 2 40-level clothes can be compounded to a 60 level clothes. \n\n#0<3>¡¼Clothes status¡½#0<0> 3 gray additional status will appear after a successful compounding. The 3 additional status can be divided into Attack class and Magic class. When you wear 3 same-class clothes, one gray status will be activated. When you wear 4 same-class clothes, the 2nc gray status will be activated. When you wear 5 same-class clothes, the last gray status will be activated.  For example: A compounded clothes with mix. Magic Attack +30.  Wearing 5 MA+ clothes, the 3 gray status will be activated. \n\nTip: Function of other 4 blank on compound panel is coming soon. ")
